Hello, Glitch Productions crew! I'm sorry if this letter takes up any time you or your associates need to create new videos on SMG4 or plan any new products for the website, but I have been watching your videos for years. I am currently 12 years old, and I have been watching your other channel, Super Meme Guardian 4, also known as Super Mario Gaming 4, for so long that I can't even remember when I started. But a few years ago, when I was a bit underage for the content on your channel, I decided to stop watching so it could not affect me in unexpected ways. But later on, I decided to come back to it because I missed watching some of the funny worlds you were known for back then, and when I came back on, I was in shock. There were so many new concepts, arcs, and characters that seemed to fit SMG4 perfectly in character and story. And when I found out about Murder Drones, a horror comedy on Glitch Productions, four days ago, I got hocked! I decided to use my allowance to buy some of your figurines for me and my two ten-year-old cousins. When we were discussing it at their house, I found out that some of the characters were limited edition. I was not around your channels 8 months ago, so me and my cousins felt a bit bad. and then more bad news struck. It turns out that since it costs more in Canadian money and I have been cheating in the US, the price increased. and now, even if the limited edition figurines were available, I would not be able to afford two sets with the limited figures. but without them, I can just barely make it with tax. I'm not saying to give me a discount or a free item (because I will have enough next week), but I am asking if, when Murder Drones Season 2 comes out, you can also re-release some of the limited edition figures. Thank you for taking the time to read this, and I hope you know you and your crew mean so much to me! Thank you, Luke! for being apart of my life  PS: I already sent this to Sheinna from Juniper Creations, and she has already told me that the limited products will not be available and that your social media is a good way to talk to you! Trees are vital. As the biggest plants on the planet, they give us oxygen, store carbon, stabilise the soil and give life to the worldâ€™s wildlife. They also provide us with the materials for tools and shelter.  Not only are trees essential for life, but as the longest living species on earth, they give us a link between the past, present and future.  Itâ€™s critical that woodlands, rainforests and trees in urban settings, such as parks, are preserved and sustainably managed across the world.  Trees benefit health The canopies of trees act as a physical filter, trapping dust and absorbing pollutants from the air. Each individual tree removes up to 1.7 kilos every year. They also provide shade from solar radiation and reduce noise.  Over 20 species of British trees and shrubs are known to have medicinal properties. The oil from birch bark, for example, has antiseptic properties.  Research shows that within minutes of being surrounded by trees and green space, your blood pressure drops, your heart rate slows and your stress levels come down.  Trees benefit the environment Trees absorb carbon dioxide as they grow and the carbon that they store in their wood helps slow the rate of global warming.  They reduce wind speeds and cool the air as they lose moisture and reflect heat upwards from their leaves. Itâ€™s estimated that trees can reduce the temperature in a city by up to 7Â°C.  Trees also help prevent flooding and soil erosion, absorbing thousands of litres of stormwater.  Trees boost wildlife Trees host complex microhabitats. When young, they offer habitation and food to amazing communities of birds, insects, lichen and fungi. When ancient, their trunks also provide the hollow cover needed by species such as bats, woodboring beetles, tawny owls and woodpeckers.  One mature oak can be home to as many as 500 different species. Richmond Park is full of such trees, which is one of the reasons it has been designated a National Nature Reserve and Site of Special Scientific Interest.  Trees strengthen communities Trees strengthen the distinctive character of a place and encourage local pride. Urban woodland can be used as an educational resource and to bring groups together for activities like walking and bird-watching. Trees are also invaluable for children to play in and discover their sense of adventure.  Trees grow the economy People are attracted to live, work and invest in green surroundings. Research shows that average house prices are 5-18% higher when properties are close to mature trees. Companies benefit from a healthier, happier workforce if there are parks and trees nearby.  Trees protect the future Soon, for the first time in history, the number of people with homes in cities will outstrip those living in the countryside. Parks and trees will become an even more vital component of urban life. We must respect them and protect them for the future.

Well, something is still weird.  Let's talk about Spider Peach and the castle remnants. Obviously Spider Peach is a nod to Calamity Ganon, but there is more.  Spider Peach first snatched Meggy and this in a tempo, that just look staged. Like a horror movie where the first guy is catched by the monster when the main character is looking away. And then Spider Peach has only eyes for SMG4. She never attacks Mario or SMG3. This isn't how a generic monster would hunt. Spider Peach serves a purpose. And whom is she serving?  The Show. He is responsible for the current state of Peachs Castle at last. And he has the capabilities to create Spider Peach.  Even further hints are the massive fourth wall breaks. All four main characters are aware, that they are in some sort of show. And the end isn't something, that Luke would plan for the end of a classic episode. It looks like a classic SMG4 ending, but here it is something else's doing. Plus, since the Genesis and Revelations Arc we know that Luke is a character in the SMG4 universe and that The Show has influence over him since he got censored by The Show.  My theory now: One Shot Wren isn't dead. In fact, they never escaped his simulation and this is revealed next week. We could also get The Meme Games 2023 (or at least the teaser), which maybe cumulates in the defeat of The Show and Wrens redemption.  What do you think?
